(function (window, document) {
    'use strict';
    var SchoolBlocksApp = {
        'initialized': false,
        'bundles': {},
        'mapLoaded': false,
        'mapCallbacks': [],
        '_cache': {}
    };

    SchoolBlocksApp.mapReady = function(callback) {
        if (SchoolBlocksApp.mapLoaded === true) {
            $(document).ready(callback);
        } else {
            SchoolBlocksApp.mapCallbacks.push(callback);
        }
    };
    
    SchoolBlocksApp.loadGoogleMap = function() {
        fallback.load({
            'google.maps': 'https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?callback=SchoolBlocksApp.googleMapCallback&key=AIzaSyAhbBaVfGPlxSdyFZKiC93rG8P6s1Yd3ko'
        });
    };

    SchoolBlocksApp.googleMapCallback = function() {
        var i;
        SchoolBlocksApp.mapLoaded = true;
        for(i = 0; i < SchoolBlocksApp.mapCallbacks.length; i++) {
            $(document).ready(SchoolBlocksApp.mapCallbacks[i]);
        }
        SchoolBlocksApp.mapCallbacks = [];
    };

    SchoolBlocksApp.ready = function (callback, libraries) {
        if (libraries === undefined) {
            libraries = ['SchoolBlocksApp.bundles.app', 'SchoolBlocksReact'];
        }

        fallback.ready(libraries, function() {
            if (SchoolBlocksApp.initialize) {
                SchoolBlocksApp.initialize();
            }
            $(document).ready(callback);
        });
    };

    SchoolBlocksApp.blocksReady = function (callback) {
        SchoolBlocksApp.ready(callback, 
            ['SchoolBlocksApp.bundles.app', 'SchoolBlocksReact', 'SchoolBlocksApp.bundles.blocks']);
    };

    
    // Add a special class that allows us to use some CSS to fix issues with modals on iOS 9
    if(/iPad|iPhone|iPod/g.test(navigator.userAgent) && !window.MSStream) {
        document.documentElement.className += "isIOS isNotAndroidChrome";
    } else if(/Android.*Chrome/g.test(navigator.userAgent) && !window.MSStream) {
        document.documentElement.className += "isNotIOS isAndroidChrome";
    } else {
        document.documentElement.className += "isNotIOS isNotAndroidChrome";
    }

    window.SchoolBlocksApp = SchoolBlocksApp;
}(window, document));

        <DIV CLASS="sb-block-container " >
        <div CLASS="sb-blockScroller sb-page-b">
    <DIV CLASS="sb-blockContent">
        <H3 class="sb-page-b-title">About Talladega County Schools</H3>
        <P class="sb-page-b-modified sb-hidden-xs">26 days ago</P>
        <div class="sb-page-b-content sb-page-body"><div class="row clearfix">
        <div class="column half flow-opposite">
            <p></p><div class="edit"><h1>TAKING THE LEAD</h1><p>The fourth largest employer in Talladega County, Alabama, the Talladega County School System has seventeen schools serving approximately 7,600 students and 1,000 employees.&nbsp; The school system and its schools have received various national and state awards including being selected as a US Department of Education Green Ribbon School System along with several schools selected as US Department of Education Green Ribbon Schools. Talladega County Schools is currently implementing a 1:1 digital device to student program, called <b>#LeadingTheWay</b>, which utilizes approximately 6,400 Chromebooks, and 1,200 iPad tablets, all of which provide 24/7 mobile access to students in grades 3-12 and daily classroom access to students in grades K-2. Each student is assigned his or her own device, which is not shared with others, making Talladega County Schools one of only a handful of districts in the state of Alabama providing this density of mobile device access.</p></div><p></p>
        </div>
        <div class="column half center">
            <img src="https://d6vze32yv269z.cloudfront.net/9c732739-17b7-4c93-bc08-23be7118361e/pages/images/img_9473-oqpk2o.jpg" class="circle" alt="Innovative district logo"></div></div><div class="row clearfix"><div class="column half">
            <p>As the district moves forward with blended learning, it continues to be recognized on both a national and state level for this work which incorporates project-based learning based on the Buck Institute for Education (BIE) model, STEAM themes, including coding, 3-D printing, robotics, and other Next Generation Science Standards. &nbsp;The Talladega County School System is a close partner with The Alliance for Excellent Education, the Digital Promise League of Innovative Schools, and was recently named a Model District by the International Center for Leadership in Education. Teachers and District Leaders are often solicited to share strategies and experience, on both a state and national level, at various conferences and organizations focused on student learning.</p>
        </div>
        <div class="column half center">
            <img src="https://d6vze32yv269z.cloudfront.net/9c732739-17b7-4c93-bc08-23be7118361e/pages/images/img_7735-sodehk.jpg" class="circle" alt="We took the pledge logo">
        </div>
    </div></div>
    </DIV>
</div>
<div class="sb-read-more text-center">
    <a href="http://www.tcboe.org/about-talladega-county-schools-9b757ce4" class="btn sb-read-more-btn sb-block-link sb-organization-color-element-bg"
       target="_self" title="Visit About Talladega County Schools Page">visit page</a>
</div>

        <H3 class="sb-page-b-title">Education Foundation Grant Winners</H3>
        <P class="sb-page-b-modified sb-hidden-xs">about 1 month ago</P>
        <div class="sb-page-b-content sb-page-body"><div class="row clearfix">
        <div class="column full">
            <p></p></div></div><div class="edit"><p align="center"><b>Talladega County Schools -- Education Foundation</b></p>  <p align="center"><b>P.O. Box 887 / Talladega, AL 35161-0887</b></p>  <p align="center"><b>January 29, 2018</b></p>  <p align="center">&nbsp;</p>  <p>The Board of Directors for the Talladega County Education Foundation announces the following school-wide and teacher grant winners:</p>  <p>&nbsp;</p>  <p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <b><u>School-wide Winners</u></b></p>  <p><u>B. B. Comer Elem.</u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; “Snap Chats”&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; $1,980.00</p>  <p><u>Childersburg Middle</u>&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; “Full STEAM Ahead at The Grid Steam Lab and Makerspace”&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; $2,000.00</p>  <p><u>Winterboro</u>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;“Fostering a Love of Reading”&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; $2,000.00</p>  <p>&nbsp;</p>  <p align="center"><b><u>Teacher Grant Winners</u></b></p>  <p><u>Comer Elem.</u>&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;         <H3 class="sb-page-b-title">Focus on Steam</H3>
        <P class="sb-page-b-modified sb-hidden-xs">about 1 month ago</P>
        <div class="sb-page-b-content sb-page-body"><div class="row clearfix">
        <div class="column half flow-opposite">
            <h3>Talladega County Brings a Focus to its STEAM Programs</h3>
            <p>Talladega County Schools has set a strong example for the rest of Alabama to follow in its forward-thinking approach to technology integration. One of the first to roll out a one-to-one digital learning environment, the District boasts a strong STEAM (STEM + Arts) program culminating in an annual Innovation Showcase – &nbsp;an event that has grown in scope and popularity with each passing year. (<a href="http://www.levelupvillage.com/alabama-school-district-brings-global-focus-steam-programs/?utm_source=email&amp;utm_medium=mailchimp&amp;utm_campaign=Newsletter_August&amp;utm_content=Talladega">Read More</a>)</p>
        </div>
        <div class="column half">
            <img src="https://d6vze32yv269z.cloudfront.net/9c732739-17b7-4c93-bc08-23be7118361e/pages/images/steam-students-a9du5l.jpg" alt="">
        </div>
    </div></div>
    </DIV>
</div>

        <P>
                        <span id="sb-footer-text" class="" data-type="textarea" data-pk="1"
                data-emptytext="Talladega County Schools provides equal opportunity in its programs, activities, and employment" data-emptyclass=""
                data-value="Title VI, IX, and Section 504 Notice of Nondiscrimination

Applicants for admission, applicants for employment, students, parents, employees, sources of referral of applicants for admission and employment, and all other professional and support organizations holding Board approved status with the Talladega County School System are hereby notified that the official policy of the Talladega County Board of Education that no person shall, on the grounds of race, color, disability, sex, religion, creed, national origin, migrant status, immigrant status, homeless status or age, be excluded from participation in, be denied the benefits of, or be subjected to discrimination under any program, activity or employment.  English as a second language (ESL) students will be guaranteed equal access to educational programming.  The Talladega County Board of Education provides equal access to the Boy Scouts and other designated youth groups. Additional services may be provided for which they qualify.

Any person having inquiries concerning the Talladega County School System’s compliance with the regulations implementing Title VI, Title IX, and Section 504 is directed to contact the person identified below who has been designated by the Talladega County School System to coordinate the systems efforts to comply with the regulations implementing Title VI, IX, and Section 504:

Mr. Kelvin Cunningham
Director of Operations
106 West South Street/P.O. Box 887/Talladega, AL
35161
(256) 315-5100

AVISO

Título VI, IX y Sección 504 Notificación de No Discriminación

Los solicitantes de admisión, los solicitantes de empleo, estudiantes, padres, empleados, fuentes de la remisión de los aspirantes para el ingreso y el empleo, y el resto de organizaciones profesionales y de apoyo a la celebración de la Junta aprobó el estado con el Sistema Escolar del Condado de Talladega queda notificado de que la política oficial de la Junta de Educación del Condado de Talladega que ninguna persona, por motivos de raza, color, discapacidad, sexo, religión, credo, origen nacional, condición de migrante, la condición de inmigrante, estado sin hogar o la edad, ser excluida de participar en, ser negado los beneficios de, o ser sujeto a discriminación bajo cualquier programa, actividad o empleo. Inglés como segundo idioma (ESL) se garantizará la igualdad de acceso a la programación educativa. Los servicios adicionales se pueden proporcionar para los que califican. La Junta de Educación del Condado de Talladega brinda igualdad de acceso a los Boy Scouts y otros grupos juveniles designados.

                Title VI, IX, and Section 504 Notice of Nondiscrimination

Applicants for admission, applicants for employment, students, parents, employees, sources of referral of applicants for admission and employment, and all other professional and support organizations holding Board approved status with the Talladega County School System are hereby notified that the official policy of the Talladega County Board of Education that no person shall, on the grounds of race, color, disability, sex, religion, creed, national origin, migrant status, immigrant status, homeless status or age, be excluded from participation in, be denied the benefits of, or be subjected to discrimination under any program, activity or employment.  English as a second language (ESL) students will be guaranteed equal access to educational programming.  The Talladega County Board of Education provides equal access to the Boy Scouts and other designated youth groups. Additional services may be provided for which they qualify.

Any person having inquiries concerning the Talladega County School System’s compliance with the regulations implementing Title VI, Title IX, and Section 504 is directed to contact the person identified below who has been designated by the Talladega County School System to coordinate the systems efforts to comply with the regulations implementing Title VI, IX, and Section 504:

Mr. Kelvin Cunningham

<script type="text/javascript">
/*<![CDATA[*/
SchoolBlocksApp.ready(function() {    var primaryNavLarge = $('#primaryNavLarge'),
        primaryNavLargeShadow = primaryNavLarge.siblings('.sb-sticky-nav-shadow');
        alertContainer = $('.sb-notification');

    if(primaryNavLarge.length > 0) {

        var alertBanner = alertContainer.find('.sb-alert-banner');
            content = $('#sb-content-canvas'),
            contentCanvasTop = content.offset().top,
            stickyNavTop = primaryNavLarge.offset().top,
            stickyNavHeight = primaryNavLarge.outerHeight(true),
            originalAlertOffsetTop = null,
            stickyAlertTop = null;
            
        var stickyNav = function() {
            var scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop(),
                navIsSticky = primaryNavLarge.hasClass('sb-sticky'),
                alertIsSticky = alertContainer.hasClass('sb-sticky')
                hasAlertBanner = alertBanner.length > 0,
                alertBannerOffset = alertBanner.offset();
                
            originalAlertOffsetTop = ((originalAlertOffsetTop === null || originalAlertOffsetTop < 0) && 
            alertBannerOffset) ? alertBannerOffset.top : originalAlertOffsetTop;
                
            if (stickyAlertTop === null) {
                stickyAlertTop = hasAlertBanner ? alertBannerOffset.top - primaryNavLarge.outerHeight() : null;
            }
            
            if (stickyAlertTop < 0) {
                stickyAlertTop = null;
            }
                
            if (scrollTop >= stickyNavTop) {
                if (!navIsSticky) {
                    primaryNavLarge.addClass('sb-sticky');
                    primaryNavLargeShadow.height(primaryNavLarge.height());
                    navIsSticky = true;
                }
            } else {
                if (navIsSticky) {
                    primaryNavLargeShadow.height(0);
                    primaryNavLarge.removeClass('sb-sticky');
                    navIsSticky = false;
                }
            }
            
            if (hasAlertBanner && stickyAlertTop !== null) {
                if (scrollTop >= stickyAlertTop) {
                    if (!alertIsSticky) {
                        alertContainer.addClass('sb-sticky');
                        alertContainer.css('top', primaryNavLarge.outerHeight(true) + 'px');
                        alertIsSticky = true;
                    }
                } else {
                    if (alertIsSticky) {
                        alertContainer.removeClass('sb-sticky');
                        alertContainer.css('top', originalAlertOffsetTop + 'px');
                        alertIsSticky = false;
                    }
                }
            }
        };
        
        var windowWidth = function() {
            return $(window).width();
        };

        if(windowWidth() > 911) {
            stickyNav();
        }

        $(window).scroll(function() {
            if(windowWidth() > 911) {
                stickyNav();
            }
        });
    }});
SchoolBlocksApp.ready(function() {    $('#userMenuButton, #mobileUserMenuButton, #userMenuButtonFooter').click(function(e){
        sb_toggleTopDrawer('#sb-user-drawer');
        e.preventDefault();
    });
        
    $('#secondaryNavSmall').on('click', '.sb-navbar-secondary-element', function(){
        if ($('#secondaryNavSmall').hasClass('mobile-open')) {
            sb_navMobileToggleMenu();
        }
    });});
